When true, the webhook automatically covers new public teams without requiring reconfiguration.' (Webhook.allPublicTeams)

The webhook will only receive payloads for events affecting these resource types.' (Webhook.resourceTypes)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Field 'Webhook.secret' description changed from 'Secret token for verifying the origin on the recipient side.' to 'A secret token used to sign webhook payloads with HMAC-SHA256, allowing the recipient to verify that the payload originated from Linear and was not tampered with. Automatically generated if not provided during creation.' (Webhook.secret)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Field 'Webhook.team' description changed from 'The team that the webhook is associated with. If null, the webhook is associated with all public teams of the organization or multiple teams.' to 'The single team that the webhook is scoped to. When null, the webhook either targets all public teams (if allPublicTeams is true), multiple specific teams (if teamIds is set), or organization-wide events.' (Webhook.team)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Field 'Webhook.teamIds' description changed from '[INTERNAL] The teams that the webhook is associated with. Used to represent a webhook that targets multiple teams, potentially in addition to all public teams of the organization.' to '[INTERNAL] An array of team IDs that the webhook is subscribed to. Used to represent a webhook that targets multiple specific teams, potentially in addition to all public teams (when allPublicTeams is also true). Null when the webhook targets a single team via teamId or all public teams only.' (Webhook.teamIds)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Field 'Webhook.url' description changed from 'Webhook URL.' to 'The destination URL where webhook payloads will be sent via HTTP POST. Null for OAuth application webhooks, which use the webhook URL configured on the OAuth client instead.' (Webhook.url)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Description 'A webhook used to send HTTP notifications over data updates.' on type 'Webhook' has changed to 'A webhook subscription that sends HTTP POST callbacks to an external URL when events occur in Linear. Webhooks can be scoped to a specific team, multiple teams, or all public teams in the organization. They support filtering by resource type (e.g., Issue, Comment, Project) and can be created either manually by users or automatically by OAuth applications. Each webhook has a signing secret for verifying payload authenticity on the recipient side.' (Webhook)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Field 'WebhookFailureEvent.executionId' description changed from 'The unique execution ID of the webhook push. This is retained between retries of the same push.' to 'A stable identifier for the webhook delivery attempt. This ID remains the same across retries of the same payload, making it useful for correlating multiple failure events that belong to the same logical delivery.' (WebhookFailureEvent.executionId)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Field 'WebhookFailureEvent.httpStatus' description changed from 'The HTTP status code returned by the recipient.' to 'The HTTP status code returned by the webhook recipient. Null if the request failed before receiving a response (e.g., DNS resolution failure, connection timeout).' (WebhookFailureEvent.httpStatus)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Field 'WebhookFailureEvent.responseOrError' description changed from 'The HTTP response body returned by the recipient or error occured.' to 'The HTTP response body returned by the recipient, or the error message if the request failed before receiving a response. Truncated to 1000 characters.' (WebhookFailureEvent.responseOrError)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Description 'Entity representing a webhook execution failure.' on type 'WebhookFailureEvent' has changed to 'A record of a failed webhook delivery attempt. Created when a webhook payload could not be successfully delivered to the destination URL, either due to an HTTP error response or a network failure. Each failure event captures the HTTP status code (if available), the response body or error message, and a stable execution ID that is shared across retries of the same delivery.' (WebhookFailureEvent)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Object type 'WorkflowDefinition' has description 'An automation workflow definition that executes a set of activities when triggered by specific events. Workflows can be scoped to a team, project, cycle, label, custom view, initiative, or user context. They are triggered by entity changes (e.g., issue status change, new comment) and can include conditions that filter which events actually execute the workflow. Activities define the actions taken, such as updating issue properties, sending notifications, or posting to Slack.' (WorkflowDefinition)

feat(schema): [non_breaking] Description 'A state in a team workflow.' on type 'WorkflowState' has changed to 'A state in a team's workflow, representing an issue status such as Triage, Backlog, Todo, In Progress, In Review, Done, or Canceled. Each team has its own set of workflow states that define the progression of issues through the team's process. Workflow states have a type that categorizes them (triage, backlog, unstarted, started, completed, canceled), a position that determines their display order, and a color for visual identification. States can be inherited from parent teams to sub-teams.' (WorkflowState)
